In this article, let's learn more about what CBDC is!\n\nWhat is CBDC?\n\nCBDC (Central Bank Digital Currency) or Central Bank Electronic Currency is a digital currency issued and managed by the Central Bank of a country.\n\nThe purpose of this currency is to replace or supplement cash and deposits in the country's financial system.\n\nCBDCs can be used like conventional currencies to pay for products and services. It can be stored in e-wallets or online bank accounts.\n\nCountries are researching and implementing CBDC as part of efforts to modernize their financial systems, reduce dependence on cash, and increase the efficiency and safety of financial transactions.\n\nWhat are the benefits of CBDC?\n\nHere are some notable benefits of CBDC:\n\nIncrease the safety of the financial system\n\nCompared to cash or traditional payment methods, CBDC is money in electronic form so it is more difficult to counterfeit. However, to ensure safety against cyber attacks or fraud, the infrastructure of the CBDC system also needs to be well protected.\n\nStrengthening the supervision capacity of the Central Bank (Central Bank)\n\nCBDC allows the Central Bank to monitor financial transactions more closely, ensuring compliance with the country's financial policies and regulations. Each CBDC coin, depending on the technology chosen, can be traced back to every transaction related to it since its issuance.\n\nThis is also different from cryptocurrencies that operate anonymously on other blockchains such as Ethereum, Bitcoin...\n\nEnhance convenience and flexibility\n\nCBDC can be used and converted across digital platforms quickly and easily. In times of crisis, having the ability to quickly convert between CBDC and traditional currencies can help optimize payment and transaction management.\n\nMinimize the impact of the crisis\n\nCBDC uses blockchain technology or other distributed technology, helping to increase transparency in financial transactions. This can help prevent fraud, money laundering and illegal financial activity, thereby reducing financial risk and creating a safer financial environment during times of crisis.\n\nCost savings\n\nCBDC can reduce costs associated with the production, distribution and management of cash, enhancing the efficiency of financial transactions. In fact, transporting and preserving cash will incur many costs. With large transactions, tallying a large amount of money costs time, effort and can cause errors in counting. In contrast, CBDC will not have these problems.\n\nWhat are the risks of CBDC?\n\nBesides the above notable benefits, CBDC also has many potential risks as follows:\n\nPrivacy and security risks\n\nCBDC is considered safer and more convenient than cash or traditional payment methods. However, it may increase the risk of personal information disclosure. It can also become a target of cyber attacks and online fraud.\n\nImpact on financial markets\n\nCBDC can lead to the movement of account balances from Commercial Banks to accounts opened at Central Banks. This could weaken the traditional role of Commercial Banks and change the overall structure of the financial system.\n\nDependence on technology\n\nCBDC depends on blockchain technology or other digital financial technologies. Therefore, it may face problems related to ensuring stable operation and adaptability to changes for both users and adopting organizations.\n\nLegal and regulatory issues\n\nImplementing a CBDC requires new legal regulations and policies to ensure its safety, security, and controllability. It can be stored in e-wallets or online bank accounts.\n\nCountries are researching and implementing CBDC as part of efforts to modernize their financial systems, reduce dependence on cash, and increase the efficiency and safety of financial transactions.\n\nWhat are the benefits of CBDC?\n\nHere are some notable benefits of CBDC:\n\nIncrease the safety of the financial system\n\nCompared to cash or traditional payment methods, CBDC is money in electronic form so it is more difficult to counterfeit. However, to ensure safety against cyber attacks or fraud, the infrastructure of the CBDC system also needs to be well protected.\n\nStrengthening the supervision capacity of the Central Bank (Central Bank)\n\nCBDC allows the Central Bank to monitor financial transactions more closely, ensuring compliance with the country's financial policies and regulations. Each CBDC coin, depending on the technology chosen, can be traced back to every transaction related to it since its issuance.\n\nThis is also different from cryptocurrencies that operate anonymously on other blockchains such as Ethereum, Bitcoin...\n\nEnhance convenience and flexibility\n\nCBDC can be used and converted across digital platforms quickly and easily. In times of crisis, having the ability to quickly convert between CBDC and traditional currencies can help optimize payment and transaction management.\n\nMinimize the impact of the crisis\n\nCBDC uses blockchain technology or other distributed technology, helping to increase transparency in financial transactions. This can help prevent fraud, money laundering and illegal financial activity, thereby reducing financial risk and creating a safer financial environment during times of crisis.\n\nCost savings\n\nCBDC can reduce costs associated with the production, distribution and management of cash, enhancing the efficiency of financial transactions. In fact, transporting and preserving cash will incur many costs. With large transactions, tallying a large amount of money costs time, effort and can cause errors in counting. In contrast, CBDC will not have these problems.\n\nWhat are the risks of CBDC?\n\nBesides the above notable benefits, CBDC also has many potential risks as follows:\n\nPrivacy and security risks\n\nCBDC is considered safer and more convenient than cash or traditional payment methods. However, it may increase the risk of personal information disclosure. It can also become a target of cyber attacks and online fraud.\n\nImpact on financial markets\n\nCBDC can lead to the movement of account balances from Commercial Banks to accounts opened at Central Banks. This could weaken the traditional role of Commercial Banks and change the overall structure of the financial system.\n\nDependence on technology\n\nCBDC depends on blockchain technology or other digital financial technologies. Therefore, it may face problems related to ensuring stable operation and adaptability to changes for both users and adopting organizations.\n\nLegal and regulatory issues\n\nImplementing a CBDC requires new legal regulations and policies to ensure its safety, security, and controllability. Market Cap v\u00e0 Fully diluted market cap\n\n=> Ch\u1eafc h\u1eb3n b\u1ea1n s\u1ebd th\u01b0\u1eddng xuy\u00ean nghe th\u1ea5y 2 kh\u00e1i ni\u1ec7m n\u00e0y: V\u1ed1n h\u00f3a th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng v\u00e0 v\u1ed1n h\u00f3a pha lo\u00e3ng ho\u00e0n to\u00e0n c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n. B\u1ea1n b\u1ecb r\u1ed1i v\u00ec 2 lo\u1ea1i v\u1ed1n h\u00f3a n\u00e0y, c\u00f9ng nhau t\u00ecm hi\u1ec3u nh\u00e9:\n\n=> Ch\u00fang ta v\u1eeba t\u00ecm hi\u1ec3u c\u00e1ch t\u00ednh marketcap = gi\u00e1 hi\u1ec7n t\u1ea1i x ngu\u1ed3n cung . Gi\u00e1 th\u00ec r\u1ea5t r\u00f5 r\u00e0ng r\u1ed3i, tuy nhi\u00ean ngu\u1ed3n cung s\u1ebd l\u00e0m b\u1ea1n b\u1ed1i r\u1ed3i v\u00ec c\u00f3 \u0111\u1ebfn 2 lo\u1ea1i ngu\u1ed3n cung : \"Ngu\u1ed3n cung l\u01b0u h\u00e0nh\" v\u00e0 \"t\u1ed5ng ngu\u1ed3n cung\"\n+ Ngu\u1ed3n cung l\u01b0u h\u00e0nh: l\u00e0 s\u1ed1 l\u01b0\u1ee3ng token \u0111ang \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u01b0u h\u00e0nh ngo\u1ea1i th\u1ecb tr\u01b0\u1eddng, n\u00f3i 1 c\u00e1ch d\u1ec5 hi\u1ec3u l\u00e0 s\u1ed1 token c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111em b\u00e1n \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c \n+ T\u1ed5ng ngu\u1ed3n cung: l\u00e0 to\u00e0n b\u1ed9 s\u1ed1 l\u01b0\u1ee3ng c\u1ee7a \u0111\u1ed3ng token \u0111\u00f3, bao g\u1ed3m c\u1ea3 nh\u1eefng token \u0111ang \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c kh\u00f3a l\u1ea1i , nh\u1eefng token \u0111ang \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c kh\u00f3a n\u00e0y s\u1ebd kh\u00f4ng th\u1ec3 \u0111em b\u00e1n \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c cho \u0111\u1ebfn khi n\u00e0o n\u00f3 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c m\u1edf kh\u00f3a\n\n=> V\u1eady c\u00e2u h\u1ecfi \u0111\u1eb7t ra l\u00e0: ch\u00fang ta c\u1ea7n quan t\u00e2m \u0111\u1ebfn market cap hay l\u00e0 fully diluted marketcap, hay n\u00f3i c\u00e1ch kh\u00e1c ch\u00fang ta c\u1ea7n quan t\u00e2m \u0111\u1ebfn cung l\u01b0u h\u00e0nh hay l\u00e0 t\u1ed5ng cung c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n. \u0110a s\u1ed1 khi h\u1ecfi c\u00e2u h\u1ecfi n\u00e0y b\u1ea1n s\u1ebd nh\u1eadn \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c c\u00e2u tr\u1ea3 l\u1eddi ch\u1ec9 c\u1ea7n quan t\u00e2m \u0111\u1ebfn cung l\u01b0u h\u00e0nh hi\u1ec7n t\u1ea1i, t\u1ee9c ch\u1ec9 c\u1ea7n quan t\u00e2m \u0111\u1ebfn market cap c\u1ee7a d\u1ef1 \u00e1n. \u0110i\u1ec1u n\u00e0y kh\u00f4ng ho\u00e0n to\u00e0n \u0111\u00fang\n\n=> N\u1ebfu b\u1ea1n l\u00e0 1 nh\u00e0 \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 ng\u1eafn h\u1ea1n, ch\u1ec9 quan t\u00e2m \u0111\u1ebfn gi\u00e1 c\u1ee7a token c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 t\u0103ng trong th\u1eddi gian ng\u1eafn hay ko, b\u1ea1n ch\u1ec9 c\u1ea7n quan t\u00e2m \u0111\u1ebfn market cap.
